20/02/2018, 08:52 - Dhruv(DTU): CHECK SUM STRING

In the beginning of his life,¬†Alan Turing (A great Computer Scientist and mathematician)¬†had made a machine which read the number from a given sequence. The numbers are written in a particular order such that each number is equal to the sum of two preceding numbers (except first and second). All the numbers of that sequence is combined together and didn't separated by any comma or space.

Example : 12 12 24 36 60 is that kind of sequence. 1212243660 is read by Turing machine which return true as each number is equal to the sum of two preceding numbers. Similarly 12 012 24 36 60 is also that kind of sequence. Hence 12012243660 will give true value.

You work is to find either written numbers will give true or false.

Input Format:

First line contains integer t as number of test cases.

Each test case contains a number without separating by comma.

Constraints:1 < t < 20 1< number < 1000000000000

Output Format:

For each test case print either true or false.

Sample Input:1 12012243660

Sample Output:true

Explanation:

Sequence = 12 012 24 36 60

21/02/2018, 17:48 - Kunal Farmah: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

void getarray(int a[][100], int n, int m){

   for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
    for(int j=0; j<m; j++)
        cin>>a[i][j];
   }
}


void printspiral(int a[][100], int n, int m) {

    int r=0;
    int c=0;

    int col=1;
    int row=0;

    while(n>0&&m>0){

    for (int i = row; i < n; i++) {
            if(a[i][c]>-32767)
        cout << a[i][c]<<", ";
        a[i][c]=-32767;
    }


        for(int j=col; j<m; j++){
                if( a[n-1][j]>-32767)
            cout<<a[n-1][j]<<", ";
            a[n-1][j]=-32767;
        }

        for (int i = n-2; i >= row; i--) {
                if(a[i][m-1]>-32767)
            cout << a[i][m-1]<<", ";
            a[i][m-1]=-32767;
        }




            for(int j=m-2; j>=col; j--){
                    if( a[r][j]>-32767)
                cout<<a[r][j]<<", ";
                a[r][j]=-32767;
            }


            ++col;
           ++row;

            ++r;
            ++c;

            --n;
            --m;

            printspiral(a, n, m);

    }


}


int main() {

 int a[100][100], n ,m;

    cin>>n>>m;

    getarray(a,n,m);

    printspiral(a,n,m);
    cout<<"END";

    return 0;
}

28/02/2018, 20:29 - Dhruv(DTU): Money Change

Given a big amount N and the array of denominations S. Assuming infinite supply of each of S = {S1,S2‚Ä¶.Sm} denominations, find the number of ways to make change for N cents.
Input Format:

First line contains an integer T denoting the total number of test cases.
For every test case, there are three lines.
First line will contain an integer 'M' denoting the size of array.
The second line contains M space-separated integers A1, A2, ‚Ä¶, Am denoting the elements of the array.
The third line contains an integer 'N' denoting the cents.
Constraints:

1 <= T <= 10
1 <= n <= 100
1 <= S[i] <= 1000
1 <= N <= 1000000

Output Format:

Print number of possible ways to make change for N cents in a new line. Since answers can be large, print answer % (1000000000 + 7).
Sample Input:

2
3
1 2 3
4
4
2 5 3 6
10

Sample Output:

4
5

Explanation:

For N = 4 and S = {1,2,3}, there are four solutions: {1,1,1,1},{1,1,2},{2,2},{1,3}. So output should be 4. For N = 10 and S = {2, 5, 3, 6}, there are five solutions: {2,2,2,2,2}, {2,2,3,3}, {2,2,6}, {2,3,5} and {5,5}. So the output should be 5.
Time Limit: 2 sec
28/02/2018, 20:30 - Dhruv(DTU): #include<iostream>
using namespace std;
void inputArr(int a[],int n){
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        cin>>a[i];
    }
}
int ans=0;
void findMaxCases(int arr[],int be,int en,int money){
    if(be>en)return;
    if(money==0)ans++;
    if(money<0)return;
    findMaxCases(arr,be,en,money-arr[be]);    
    findMaxCases(arr,be+1,en,money-arr[be]);
    
}



int main() {
int t;
cin>>t;
for (int i=0;i<t;i++) {
    int n,a[100],money;
    cin>>n;
    inputArr(a,n);
    cin>>money;
    findMaxCases(a,0,n-1,money);
    cout<<ans<<endl;
    ans=0;
}
    
}

int postfix(string exp){

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

if(valid) {

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

continue;

}

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

int val1 = postfix.top();

postfix.pop();

‚Äã

int val2 = postfix.top();

postfix.pop();

‚Äã

postfix.push(val1 + val2);

‚Äã

}

‚Äã

‚Äã

postfix.pop();

‚Äã

postfix.pop();

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

}

‚Äã

‚Äã

postfix.pop();

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

using namespace std;

‚Äã

class TreeNode{

public:

int data;

TreeNode *left, *right;

TreeNode(int x){

data = x;

left = NULL;

right = NULL;

}

};

‚Äã

int linsearch( int arr[], int size, int n){

int index;

‚Äã

for ( index=0; index<size; index++){

if (arr[index] == n)

return index;

}

‚Äã

return -1;

‚Äã

}

‚Äã

void preOrderPrint(TreeNode* root){

‚Äã

if (root == NULL) return;

‚Äã

cout << root->data << " ";

‚Äã

preOrderPrint(root->left);

preOrderPrint(root->right);

‚Äã

}

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

TreeNode* createTree(int post[], int post_beg, int post_end, int in[], int in_beg, int in_end, int pindex){

‚Äã

‚Äã

if(in_beg>in_end)

return NULL;

‚Äã

int root = post[pindex];// the last element in postorder is root;

‚Äã

--pindex; // decrementing the last index

‚Äã

‚Äã

auto treeroot = new TreeNode(root); // making root

‚Äã

‚Äã

if(in_beg==in_end) // if no children are there

‚Äã

return treeroot;

‚Äã

‚Äã

int root_index = linsearch(in,in_end,root); // searching for root in the inorder

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

‚Äã

// int len_leftpost= root_index - in_beg; // finding length of left postorder

‚Äã

‚Äã

treeroot->left = createTree(post, post_beg, root_index-1, in,in_beg, root_index-1 , pindex); // doing it recursively for left subtree

treeroot->right= createTree(post,root_index+1, post_end, in, root_index+1, in_end , pindex); // doing it recursively fot right subtree

‚Äã

return treeroot;

‚Äã

‚Äã

}

06/02/2020, 14:53 - Dhruv(DTU): #include <bits/stdc++.h>
#include <ext/pb_ds/assoc_container.hpp> 
#include <ext/pb_ds/detail/standard_policies.hpp>
#include <ext/rope>

using namespace std;
using namespace __gnu_pbds;
using namespace __gnu_cxx;

#define IOS ios::sync_with_stdio(0); cin.tie(0); cout.tie(0);
#define endl "\n"
#define long long long 

#define TRACE
#ifdef TRACE
#define trace(...) __f(#__VA_ARGS__, __VA_ARGS__)
    template <typename Arg1>
    void __f(const char* name, Arg1&& arg1){
        cout << name << " : " << arg1 << endl;
        //use cerr if u want to display at the bottom
    }
    template <typename Arg1, typename... Args>
    void __f(const char* names, Arg1&& arg1, Args&&... args){
        const char* comma = strchr(names + 1, ','); cout.write(names, comma - names) << " : " << arg1<<" | ";__f(comma+1, args...);
    }
#else
#define trace(...)
#endif

typedef trie<string,null_type,trie_string_access_traits<>,pat_trie_tag,trie_prefix_search_node_update> pref_trie;
typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;
typedef cc_hash_table<long int,long int, hash<long int>, equal_to<long int>, direct_mask_range_hashing<long int>, 
hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;

class BIT{
    ht vec;
    public:
        BIT(){
            
        }

        void update(long int idx, long int val){
            for(; idx < 1001; idx += idx & (-idx))
                vec[idx] += val;
        }

        long int query(long int b){
            long int result = 0;
            while(b){
                result += vec[b];
                b -= b & (-b);
            }
            return result;
        }
};


int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
      long int n;
      cin>>n;

      BIT tree;
      long int ans = 0;
      vector<long int> v(n);
      for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
         cin>>v[i];

      for(long int i = n - 1; i >= 0; i--){
         long int val = tree.query(v[i] - 1);
         ans += val;
         tree.update(v[i],1);
      }

      if(ans % 2 == 0)
         cout<<"YES\n";
      else
         cout<<"NO\n";
   }
   return 0;
}

Greetings from Wipro!

 At various intervals in our lives, we encounter new milestones ‚Äì beyond which lies a novel and unfamiliar path to be embarked upon. What brings a sense of familiarity and comfort on this path is, very often, the quick wise words from parents, vivid experiences of older siblings, exciting narratives from friends or tales of caution from elders. Not only do these experiences but also the relator themselves guide you and help you brace the new journey with ease.

With the similar sentiment at its core, we are immensely proud to launch the TURBO Internship Programme 2020. The objective of this programme is to deliver a great learning experience encouraging the students, alongside a mentor, to explore and master the alpha & omega of technology in the corporate world.

The programme will provide you with a wholesome understanding of a real-world where new technological advancements occur every hour. During the course of your internship, you will be exposed to real-time business problems. You would be compelled to challenge and test the concepts and theories learnt in your academic life and create innovative yet real and workable solutions.

Throughout the programme, you will be in touch with one of the Wipro leaders, who would play a key role in your development as your mentor. #define IOS ios::sync_with_stdio(0); cin.tie(0); cout.tie(0);

#ifdef TRACE
#define trace(...) __f(#__VA_ARGS__, __VA_ARGS__)
    template <typename Arg1>
    void __f(const char* name, Arg1&& arg1){
        cout << name << " : " << arg1 << endl;
        //use cerr if u want to display at the bottom
    }
    template <typename Arg1, typename... Args>
    void __f(const char* names, Arg1&& arg1, Args&&... args){
        const char* comma = strchr(names + 1, ','); cout.write(names, comma - names) << " : " << arg1<<" | ";__f(comma+1, args...);
    }
#else
#define trace(...)
#endif

typedef trie<string,null_type,trie_string_access_traits<>,pat_trie_tag,trie_prefix_search_node_update> pref_trie;
typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;
typedef cc_hash_table<long int,long int, hash<long int>, equal_to<long int>, direct_mask_range_hashing<long int>, 
hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;


int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
   	long int a,b;
   	cin>>a>>b;

   	if(a == b)
   		cout<<"0\n";
   	else if(a > b){
   		long int par = a & 1;
   		long int par2 = b & 1;
   		if(par == par2)
   			cout<<"1\n";
   		else
   			cout<<"2\n";
   	}
   	else{
   		long int par = a & 1;
   		long int par2 = b & 1;
   		if(par != par2)
   			cout<<"1\n";
   		else
   			cout<<"2\n";	
   	}
   }
   return 0;
}

typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;
typedef cc_hash_table<long int,long int, hash<long int>, equal_to<long int>, direct_mask_range_hashing<long int>, 
hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;


int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
   	long int n,m;
   	cin>>n>>m;

   	vector<long int> v(n);
   	for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
   		cin>>v[i];

   	ordered_set os;
   	for(long int i = 0; i < m; i++){
   		long int x;
   		cin>>x;
   		os.insert(x-1);
   	}

   	for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
   		for(long int j = 0; j < n - 1; j++){
   			if(v[j] >= v[j+1] && os.find(j) != os.end()){
   				swap(v[j],v[j+1]);
   			}
   		}
   	}


   	long int me = -1e10;
   	bool done = true;

   	for(long int i = 0; i < n;i++){
   		if(v[i] >= me)
   			me = v[i];
   		else
   			done = false;
   	}


   	if(done)
   		cout<<"YES\n";
   	else
   		cout<<"NO\n";

   }

   return 0;
}

hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;


int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   
	long int t;
	cin>>t;

	while(t--){
		long int n,m;
		cin>>n>>m;

		map<char,long int> combo;
		
		string s;
		cin>>s;

		vector<long int> breaks;
		for(long int i = 0; i < m; i++){
			long int x;
			cin>>x;
			x--;
			breaks.push_back(x);
		}

		sort(breaks.begin(),breaks.end());
		for(auto ele : s)
			combo[ele]++;

		map<char,long int> temp;
		long int idx = 0;
		temp[s[0]]++;

		for(long int i  = 0; i < n; i++){

			if(idx < breaks.size() && i == breaks[idx]){
				for(char c = 'a'; c <= 'z'; c++)
					combo[c] += temp[c];
				idx++;
				i--;

				// for(auto ele : combo)
				// 	cout<<ele.first<<" "<<ele.second<<endl;
				// cout<<endl;

				continue;
			}
			if(i < n)
			temp[s[i + 1]]++;

			if(idx == breaks.size())
				break;
		}

		for(auto ele : combo)
			cout<<ele.second<<" ";
		cout<<endl;
	}   
   return 0;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
      long int n;
      cin>>n;

      vector<long int> v(n);
      for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
         cin>>v[i];

      long int mine = *min_element(v.begin(),v.end());

      bool done = true;
      for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
         v[i] -= mine;
         if(v[i] % 2){
            done = false;
            break;
         }
      }

      if(done)
         cout<<"YES\n";
      else
         cout<<"NO\n";
   }
   return 0;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
      long int n;
      cin>>n;

      vector<long int> v(n);
      for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
         cin>>v[i];

      unordered_map<long int,long int> umap;

      bool done = false;
      for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
         if(umap[v[i]]){
            long int last = umap[v[i]];
            long int current = i + 1;
            if(current - last >= 2){
               done = true;
               break;
            }
         }
         else{
            umap[v[i]] = i + 1;
         }
      }
   
      if(done)
         cout<<"YES\n";
      else
         cout<<"NO\n";
   }  

   return 0;
}

   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
      string s;
      cin>>s;
      s = 'R' + s;
      s.push_back('R');

      long int distance = 0, last = -1;

      for(long int i = 0; i < s.size(); i++){
         if(s[i] == 'L')
            continue;
         else{
            distance = max(distance,i - last);
            last = i;
         }
      }

      cout<<distance<<endl;
   }  

   return 0;
}

using namespace __gnu_cxx;

#define IOS ios::sync_with_stdio(0); cin.tie(0); cout.tie(0);

#define long long long

    template <typename Arg1>

        cout << name << " : " << arg1 << endl;
        //use cerr if u want to display at the bottom
    }
    template <typename Arg1, typename... Args>
    void __f(const char* names, Arg1&& arg1, Args&&... args){
        const char* comma = strchr(names + 1, ','); cout.write(names, comma - names) << " : " << arg1<<" | ";__f(comma+1, args...);

#define trace(...)
#endif

typedef trie<string,null_type,trie_string_access_traits<>,pat_trie_tag,trie_prefix_search_node_update> pref_trie;
typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;
typedef cc_hash_table<long int,long int, hash<long int>, equal_to<long int>, direct_mask_range_hashing<long int>, 
hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;

class BIT{
    unordered_map<long int,long int> vec;
    public:
        void update(long int idx, long int val){
            for(; idx < 2e9 + 5; idx += idx & (-idx))
                vec[idx] += val;
        }

        long int query(long int b){
            long int result = 0;
            while(b){
                result += vec[b];
                b -= b & (-b);
            }
            return result;
        }
};

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   
   long int n;
   cin>>n;

   vector<pair<long int,long int>> v(n);
   vector<long int> diff;

   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
      cin>>v[i].first;

   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
      cin>>v[i].second;

   for(long int i= 0; i < n; i++)
      diff.push_back(v[i].first - v[i].second);

   sort(diff.begin(),diff.end());

   // for(auto ele : diff)
   //    cout<<ele<<" ";
   // cout<<endl;

   BIT tree;
   for(auto ele : diff)
      tree.update(ele + 1e9 + 1,1);
   

   sort(v.begin(),v.end(),[](pair<long int,long int> a,pair<long int,long int> b){
      long int differ1 = a.first - a.second;
      long int differ2 = b.first - b.second;
      
      return differ1 < differ2;    
   });

   // for(auto ele : v)
   //    cout<<ele.first<<" "<<ele.second<<endl;

   long int ans = 0;
   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
      long int differ = v[i].second  - v[i].first;
      long int calc = tree.query(differ + 1e9 + 1);
      // trace(calc,differ,n-calc-i);
      tree.update(-differ + 1e9 + 1,-1);
      if(differ < 0)
         calc = n - i - n + i + 1;
      ans += (n - calc - i);
   }

   cout<<ans;
   return 0;
}

        const char* comma = strchr(names + 1, ','); cout.write(names, comma - names) << " : " << arg1<<" | ";__f(comma+1, args...);

typedef trie<string,null_type,trie_string_access_traits<>,pat_trie_tag,trie_prefix_search_node_update> pref_trie;
typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;
typedef cc_hash_table<long int,long int, hash<long int>, equal_to<long int>, direct_mask_range_hashing<long int>, 
hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;

long int dp[2005][2005];

long int solve(long int time,long int idx,long int &l,long int &r,long int &h,long int &n,vector<long int> &v){
   if(idx == n)
      return 0;

   if(dp[time][idx] != -1)
      return dp[time][idx];

   time %= h;
   long int score = 0;
   score += max(solve((time + v[idx]) % h,idx + 1,l,r,h,n,v) + (((time + v[idx]) % h <= r && (time + v[idx]) % h >= l)) , solve((time + v[idx] - 1) % h, idx + 1,l ,r, h, n, v) + (((time + v[idx] - 1) % h <= r && (time + v[idx] - 1) % h >= l)));
   return dp[time][idx] =  score; 
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   long int n,h,l,r;
   cin>>n>>h>>l>>r;

   memset(dp,-1,sizeof(dp));
   vector<long int> v(n);
   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
      cin>>v[i];

   cout<<solve(0,0,l,r,h,n,v);  

   return 0;
}

typedef trie<string,null_type,trie_string_access_traits<>,pat_trie_tag,trie_prefix_search_node_update> pref_trie;
typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;
typedef cc_hash_table<long int,long int, hash<long int>, equal_to<long int>, direct_mask_range_hashing<long int>, 
hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;

class BIT{
    unordered_map<long int,long int> vec;
    public:
        void update(long int idx, long int val){
            for(; idx < 2e9 + 5; idx += idx & (-idx))
                vec[idx] += val;
        }

        long int query(long int b){
            long int result = 0;
            while(b){
                result += vec[b];
                b -= b & (-b);
            }
            return result;
        }
};

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   
   long int n;
   cin>>n;

   vector<pair<long int,long int>> v(n);
   vector<long int> diff;

   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
      cin>>v[i].first;

   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
      cin>>v[i].second;

   for(long int i= 0; i < n; i++)
      diff.push_back(v[i].first - v[i].second);

   sort(diff.begin(),diff.end());

   // for(auto ele : diff)
   //    cout<<ele<<" ";
   // cout<<endl;

   BIT tree;
   for(auto ele : diff)
      tree.update(ele + 1e9 + 1,1);
   

   sort(v.begin(),v.end(),[](pair<long int,long int> a,pair<long int,long int> b){
      long int differ1 = a.first - a.second;
      long int differ2 = b.first - b.second;
      
      return differ1 < differ2;    
   });

   // for(auto ele : v)
   //    cout<<ele.first<<" "<<ele.second<<endl;

   long int ans = 0;
   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
      long int differ = v[i].second  - v[i].first;
      long int calc = tree.query(differ + 1e9 + 1);
      // trace(calc,differ,n-calc-i);
      tree.update(-differ + 1e9 + 1,-1);
      if(differ < 0)
         calc = n - i - n + i + 1;
      ans += (n - calc - i);
   }

   cout<<ans;
   return 0;
}

	vector<bool> primeSieve(int n){
	    std::vector<bool> p(n+1,false);
		p[0]=p[1]=0;
		p[2]=1;
	    for(int i=3;i<=n;i+=2){
	        p[i] = 1;
	    }
	    for(int i=3;i<=sqrt(n);i+=2){
	        if(p[i]){
	            for(int j=i*i;j<=n;j+=2*i){
	                p[j] = 0;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    return p;
	}
	
	ll power(ll x, ll y, ll m){
		if(y==0)
			return 1;
		ll smallpower = power(x,y/2,m);
		smallpower = smallpower%m;
		smallpower = (smallpower*smallpower)%m;
		if(y&1)
	         return (x*smallpower)%m;
		else
			return (smallpower%m);
	}
	
	int bsearch(vector<int> a, int b, int e, int x){
		if(b>e)return -1;
		int mid = (b+e)/2;
		if(a[mid]==x)return mid;
		else if(a[mid]>x)return bsearch(a,b,mid-1,x);
		else return bsearch(a,mid+1,e,x);
	}

// kunalfarmah98@gmail.com

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

#define RTIME ((double)clock()/(double)CLOCKS_PER_SEC)
#define IOS ios_base::sync_with_stdio(false);cin.tie(0);cout.tie(0);

#define Mod 1000000007

typedef long long int ll;
typedef unsigned long long int ull;
typedef long double ld;
typedef pair < int, int > pii;
typedef pair < ll, ll > pll;
typedef vector<int> vi;
typedef vector<vi> vvi;
typedef vector<bool> vb;
typedef queue<int> qi;
typedef complex<double> base;

const ld pi = 3.141592653589793238462643383;
const double PI = 3.141592653589793;

template<class T>
using max_pq = priority_queue<T>;
template<class T>
using min_pq = priority_queue<T,vector<T>,greater<T>>;


vector<bool> primeSieve(int n){
    std::vector<bool> p(n+1,false);
    p[0]=p[1]=0;
    p[2]=1;
    for(int i=3;i<=n;i+=2){
        p[i] = 1;
    }
    for(int i=3;i<=sqrt(n);i+=2){
        if(p[i]){
            for(int j=i*i;j<=n;j+=2*i){
                p[j] = 0;
            }
        }
    }
    return p;
}

ll power(ll x, ll y, ll m){
    if(y==0)
        return 1;
    ll smallpower = power(x,y/2,m);
    smallpower = smallpower%m;
    smallpower = (smallpower*smallpower)%m;
    if(y&1)
        return (x*smallpower)%m;
    else
        return (smallpower%m);
}



int main(){



    int t;
    cin>>t;
    while(t--){
        int n;
        cin>>n;
        int a[n];
        for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
            cin>>a[i];
        }
        int f;
        int res;
        ll ans=1;
        for(int i=1; i<n; i++){
                f=a[i-1];
                res = a[i];
            while(f || res){
                int fl = f&1;
                int rl = res&1;
                if(fl && rl){
                    ans*=2;
                    ans%=Mod;
                }
                f=(f>>1);
                res = (res>>1);
            }
        }

        cout<<ans%Mod<<endl;

    }

    return 0;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
 	long int t;
 	cin>>t;

 	while(t--){
 		long int n;
		cin>>n;
		
		vector<long int> a(n);
		
		for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++) 
			cin>>a[i];
		
		long int mod = 1e9 + 7, ans = 1;
		bool poss = true;
		
		for(long int i = 1; i < n; i++){
			long int count = 0;
			for(long int j=0; j < 31; j++){
				if(((1<<j) & a[i-1]) && !((1<<j) & a[i])){
					poss = false;
					break;
				}
				if(( (1<<j) & a[i-1] ) && ((1<<j) & a[i])){
					count++;
				}				
			}
			for(long int j=0;j < count;j++)
				ans = (ans % mod * 2) % mod;
		}
		if(!poss) 
			cout <<"0"<<endl;
		else 
			cout<<ans<<endl;
	}	  

   return 0;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
   	long int minRotations = 0, maxRotations = 1e10;
   	long int n;
   	cin>>n;

   	vector<long int> v(n);
   	for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
   		cin>>v[i];

   	long int e = *max_element(v.begin(),v.end());

   	for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
   		if(v[i] == e){
   			if(i >= n / 2)
   				minRotations = max(minRotations,0LL);
   			else 
   				minRotations = max(minRotations, n/2 - i);

   			if(i >= n / 2)
   				maxRotations = min(maxRotations, n - i - 1);
   			else 
   				maxRotations = min(maxRotations, n/2 - i + n/2 - 1);
   		}
   		if(minRotations > maxRotations)
   			break;
   	}
   	if(maxRotations - minRotations > 0)
   		cout<<maxRotations - minRotations + 1<<endl;
   	else
   		cout<<"0\n";
   }
   return 0;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
   	long int minRotations = 0, maxRotations = 1e10;
   	long int n;
   	cin>>n;

   	vector<long int> v(n);
   	for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
   		cin>>v[i];

   	long int e = *max_element(v.begin(),v.end());

   	for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
   		if(v[i] == e){
   			if(i >= n / 2)
   				minRotations = max(minRotations,0LL);
   			else 
   				minRotations = max(minRotations, n/2 - i - 1);

   			if(i >= n / 2)
   				maxRotations = min(maxRotations, n - i - 1);
   			else 
   				maxRotations = min(maxRotations, n/2 - i + n/2 - 1);
   		}
   		if(minRotations > maxRotations)
   			break;
   	}
   	if(maxRotations - minRotations > 0)
   		cout<<maxRotations - minRotations<<endl;
   	else

   }

	vector<bool> primeSieve(int n){
	    std::vector<bool> p(n+1,false);
		p[0]=p[1]=0;
		p[2]=1;
	    for(int i=3;i<=n;i+=2){
	        p[i] = 1;
	    }
	    for(int i=3;i<=sqrt(n);i+=2){
	        if(p[i]){
	            for(int j=i*i;j<=n;j+=2*i){
	                p[j] = 0;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    return p;
	}
	
	ll power(ll x, ll y, ll m){
		if(y==0)
			return 1;
		ll smallpower = power(x,y/2,m);
		smallpower = smallpower%m;
		smallpower = (smallpower*smallpower)%m;
		if(y&1)
	         return (x*smallpower)%m;
		else
			return (smallpower%m);
	}

typedef trie<string,null_type,trie_string_access_traits<>,pat_trie_tag,trie_prefix_search_node_update> pref_trie;
typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;
typedef cc_hash_table<long int,long int, hash<long int>, equal_to<long int>, direct_mask_range_hashing<long int>, 
hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;

vector <long int> primes; 
const long int MOD = 1e9 + 7;
const long int MAX = 1e5;  

void sieve(){ 
    bool isComposite[MAX] = {false}; 
    for (long int i=2; i*i<=MAX; i++) 
    { 
        if (isComposite[i]==false) 
            for (int j=2; j*i<=MAX; j++) 
                isComposite[i*j] = true; 
    } 
  
    for (long int i=2; i<=MAX; i++) 
        if (isComposite[i]==false) 
            primes.push_back(i); 
} 
   
long int LCM(long int n){ 
    long int lcm = 1; 
    for (long int i=0; i < primes.size() && primes[i] <= n; i++){ 
        long int pp = primes[i]; 
        while (pp*primes[i] <= n) 
            pp = pp *primes[i]; 
  
        lcm *= pp; 
        lcm %= MOD; 
    } 
    return lcm; 
} 
 

vector<long int> getFactors(long int num){
  vector<long int> factors;
  long int idx = 0;
  while(num > 1){
    while(num % primes[idx] == 0){
      num /= primes[idx];
      factors.push_back(primes[idx]);
    }
    idx++;
  }
  return factors;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
    long int t;
    cin>>t;
    sieve();

    while(t--){
      long int n,m;
      cin>>n>>m;

      long int val = LCM(m);
      vector<long int> v(n);
      for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        cin>>v[i];

      long int lcm = v[0];

      for(long int i = 1; i < n; i++){
        long int g = __gcd(lcm,v[i]);
        lcm = (lcm * v[i]) / g;
      }

      long int ans = 1;
        
      vector<long int> fact1 = getFactors(val);
      vector<long int> fact2 = getFactors(lcm);
      
      // trace(val);
      // for(auto ele : fact1)
      //   cout<<ele<<" ";
      // cout<<endl;

      // trace(lcm);
      // for(auto ele : fact2)
      //   cout<<ele<<" ";
      // cout<<endl;
      

      sort(fact1.rbegin(),fact1.rend());

      multiset<long int> fact;
      
        for(auto ele : fact2)
          fact.insert(ele);

      for(auto ele : fact1){
        if(fact.find(ele) != fact.end()){
          fact.erase(fact.find(ele));
          continue;
        }
        if(ans * ele <= m){
          ans *= ele;      
        }
      }

      cout<<ans<<endl;
    }

   return 0;
}

long int getNum(string a){
  stringstream ss(a);
  long int num;
  ss>>num;
  return num;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
  long int t;
  cin>>t;

  while(t--){
    string a,b;
    cin>>a>>b;

    long int ans = getNum(a) + getNum(b);
    for(long int i = 0; i < a.size(); i++){
      for(long int j = 0; j < b.size(); j++){
        swap(a[i],b[j]);
        ans = max(ans,getNum(a) + getNum(b));
        swap(a[i],b[j]);
      }
    }


    cout<<ans<<endl;
  }  

   return 0;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 //    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
 //        freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
 //        freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
 //    #endif
  long int t;
  cin>>t;

  while(t--){
    string s;
    cin>>s;

    long int n,x;
    cin>>n>>x;

    unordered_map<char,long int> umap;
    long int good = 0, ans = 0;

    for(auto ele : s){
      umap[ele]++;
      if(umap[ele] > x && good < n){
        umap[ele]--;
        good++;
        continue;
      }
      else if(umap[ele] > x)
        break;
      ans++;
    }
    cout<<ans<<endl;
  }  

   return 0;
}

16/04/2020, 17:40 - Kunal Farmah: class Solution {
public:
    
    int cnt(vector<vector<int>>& grid, int x, int y, int dx, int dy,vector<vector<bool>>& visited, bool cancel){
        if(x==dx && y==dy && !visited[x][y] && grid[x][y]!=-1){
            cancel = false;
            return 1;
        }
        if(x<0 || x>dx || y<0 || y>dy || visited[x][y] || grid[x][y]==-1){
            cancel  = true;
            return 0;
        }
        
        int l=0,r=0,u=0,d=0;
        visited[x][y]=true;
        l = cnt(grid,x,y-1,dx,dy,visited,cancel);
       // if(cancel)visited[x][y]=false;
        //visited[x][y]=true;
        r = cnt(grid,x,y+1,dx,dy,visited,cancel);
        //if(cancel)visited[x][y]=false;
       // visited[x][y]=true;
        u = cnt(grid,x-1,y,dx,dy,visited,cancel);
       // if(cancel)visited[x][y]=false;
        //visited[x][y]=true;
        d = cnt(grid,x+1,y,dx,dy,visited,cancel);
        if(cancel)visited[x][y]=false;

        
        return l+r+u+d;
            
    }
    int uniquePathsIII(vector<vector<int>>& grid) {
        int m = grid.size();
        int n = grid[0].size();
        
        int x,y,dx,dy;
        for(int i=0; i<m; i++){
            for(int j=0; j<n; j++){
                if(grid[i][j]==1){
                    x=i;
                    y=j;
                }
                else if(grid[i][j]==2){
                    dx=i;
                    dy=j;
                }
            }
        }
        
        vector<vector<bool>>visited(m,vector<bool>(n,false));
        bool c =false;
        return cnt(grid,x,y,dx,dy,visited,c);
    }
};

16/04/2020, 18:08 - Dhruv(DTU): class Solution {
public:
    long int DFS(vector<vector<int>>& g,long int i,long int j,long int s, long int steps) {
  
        if (i < 0 || j < 0 || i >= g.size() || j >= g[0].size() || g[i][j] == -1) 
            return 0;
  
        if (g[i][j] == 2) 
            return s == steps ? 1 : 0;
  
        g[i][j] = -1;
  
        long int paths = DFS(g, i + 1, j, s + 1, steps) + 
                         DFS(g, i - 1, j, s + 1, steps) + 
                         DFS(g, i, j + 1, s + 1, steps) + 
                         DFS(g, i, j - 1, s + 1, steps);
        g[i][j] = 0;  
        return paths;

    }
    int uniquePathsIII(vector<vector<int>>& g) {
  
        long int initialX = 0, initialY = 0, steps = 0;

        for (auto i = 0; i < g.size(); ++i)
            for (auto j = 0; j < g[0].size(); ++j) {
      
                if (g[i][j] == 1) 
                    initialX = i, initialY = j;
      
                if (g[i][j] != -1) 
                    ++steps;
            }
        return DFS(g, initialX, initialY, 1, steps);
    }
};

	#include <bits/stdc++.h>
	using namespace std;

	#define RTIME ((double)clock()/(double)CLOCKS_PER_SEC)
	#define IOS ios_base::sync_with_stdio(false);cin.tie(0);cout.tie(0);
	
	#define MOD 1000000007
	
	typedef long long int ll;
	typedef unsigned long long int ull;
	typedef long double ld;
	typedef pair < int, int > pii;
	typedef pair < ll, ll > pll;
	typedef vector<int> vi;
	typedef vector<vi> vvi;
	typedef vector<bool> vb;
	typedef queue<int> qi;
	typedef complex<double> base;
	
	const ld pi = 3.141592653589793238462643383; 
	const double PI = 3.141592653589793;
	
	template<class T>
	using max_pq = priority_queue<T>;
	template<class T>
	using min_pq = priority_queue<T,vector<T>,greater<T>>; 
	
	
	vector<bool> primeSieve(int n){
	    std::vector<bool> p(n+1,false);
		p[0]=p[1]=0;
		p[2]=1;
	    for(int i=3;i<=n;i+=2){
	        p[i] = 1;
	    }
	    for(int i=3;i<=sqrt(n);i+=2){
	        if(p[i]){
	            for(int j=i*i;j<=n;j+=2*i){
	                p[j] = 0;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    return p;
	}
	
	ll power(ll x, ll y, ll m){
		if(y==0)
			return 1;
		ll smallpower = power(x,y/2,m);
		smallpower = smallpower%m;
		smallpower = (smallpower*smallpower)%m;
		if(y&1)
	         return (x*smallpower)%m;
		else
			return (smallpower%m);
	}
	
	
	
	int main(){
		IOS;
		#ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
   			freopen("input.txt", "r", stdin);
    		freopen("output.txt", "w", stdout);
		#endif
		

		int t;
		cin>>t;
		while(t--){
			int n,c;
			cin>>n>>c;
			
			ll ans = c;
			ll prev = c; 
			ll prevc = c;
			ll val = c;
			//cout<<val<<endl;
			for(int i=2; i<=n; i++){
				c*=prev;
				c%=MOD;
				val = power(c,2*i-1,MOD);
				//cout<<val<<endl;
				ans+=val;
				ans%=MOD;
				prev=val;
			}
			cout<<ans<<endl;
			
		}
	
		return 0;
	}

const long int MOD = 1e9 + 7;

	template <typename T>
	T modpow(T base, T exp, T modulus) {
  	base = base % modulus;
  	T result = 1;
  	while (exp > 0) {
    	if (exp % 2 == 1) result = (result * base) % modulus;
    	base = (base * base) % modulus;
    	exp = exp/2;
  	}
  	return result;
	}
	

int main(){
   IOS;
 /*    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
         freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
         freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
     #endif */
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
   		long int n,a;
   		cin>>n>>a;

   		long int current = a;
		long int ans = 0;

		for(long int i = 1; i <= n; i++){
			long int give = 2*i - 1;
			long int total = modpow(current,give,MOD);
			ans = (ans + total) % MOD;
			current = (total * current) % MOD;
		}

		cout<<ans<<endl;   		
   }
   return 0;
}

     #endif */
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
    string a,b;
    cin>>a>>b;

    vector<long int> dp(a.size() + 2);

    for(long int i = 0; i < a.size(); i++){
      if(a[i] == b[i])
        continue;
      dp[i + 1] = dp[i] + 1;
    }

    long int sum = 0, cnt = 0;
    for(long int i = 0; i < dp.size() - 1; i++)
      if(dp[i+1] == 0 && dp[i]){
        sum += dp[i];
        cnt++;
      }

    cout<<sum * cnt<<endl;
   }
   return 0;
}

int main(){
   IOS;
 /*    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
         freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
         freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
     #endif */
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
    long int n,k;
    cin>>n>>k;

    vector<long int> v(n);

    for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        cin>>v[i];

    vector<long int> range(2*k + 2, 0);

    for(long int i = 0; i < n / 2; i++){
      long int smallOne = min(v[i],v[n - i - 1]);
      long int bigOne = max(v[i], v[n - i - 1]);
      
      range[v[i] + v[n - i - 1]] -= 1;
      range[v[i] + v[n - i - 1] + 1] += 1;
      range[smallOne + 1]--;
      range[bigOne + k + 1]++; 
    }

    long int ans = 1e10;
    
      long int delta = 0;
    for(long int i = 2; i <= 2*k; i++){
      delta += range[i];
      ans = min(ans, n + delta);
    }


    cout<<ans<<endl;

   }

   return 0;
}

vector<bool> primeSieve(int n){
    std::vector<bool> p(n+1,false);
    p[0]=p[1]=0;
    p[2]=1;
    for(int i=3;i<=n;i+=2){
        p[i] = 1;
    }
    for(int i=3;i<=sqrt(n);i+=2){
        if(p[i]){
            for(int j=i*i;j<=n;j+=2*i){
                p[j] = 0;
            }
        }
    }
    return p;
}

ll power(ll x, ll y, ll m){
    if(y==0)
        return 1;
    ll smallpower = power(x,y/2,m);
    smallpower = smallpower%m;
    smallpower = (smallpower*smallpower)%m;
    if(y&1)
        return (x*smallpower)%m;
    else
        return (smallpower%m);
}

bool canplace(char a[25][25], int x, int y, int n){
    int dirx[8] = {0,1,0,-1,1,-1,1,-1};
    int diry[8] = {1,0,-1,0,1,1,-1,-1};

    for(int i=0; i<8; i++){
        if(x+dirx[i]>=0 && x+dirx[i]<n && y+diry[i]>=0 && y+diry[i]<n){
            if(a[x+dirx[i]][y+diry[i]]=='K')return false;
            // checking only 1 king in current column
            for(int j=0; j<n; j++){
                if(j!=x && a[j][y]=='K')return false;
            }
        }
    }
    return true;

}
int ans=0;
bool nkings(char a[25][25], int r,  int n){
    if(r==n){
        ++ans;
        return false;
    }
    for(int c=0; c<n; c++){
        if(canplace(a,r,c,n)){
            a[r][c]='K';

            bool further  = nkings(a,r+1,n);
            if(further)return true;

            a[r][c]=' ';
        }
    }

    return false;
}


int main(){
//    IOS;
//#ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
//    freopen("input.txt", "r", stdin);
//    freopen("output.txt", "w", stdout);
//#endif


    int n;
    cin>>n;

    char a[25][25];
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++)
        for(int j=0; j<n; j++)
            a[i][j]=' ';

    nkings(a,0,n);
    cout<<ans<<endl;




    return 0;
}

	template<class T>

	vector<bool> primeSieve(int n){
	    std::vector<bool> p(n+1,false);
		p[0]=p[1]=0;
		p[2]=1;
	    for(int i=3;i<=n;i+=2){
	        p[i] = 1;
	    }
	    for(int i=3;i<=sqrt(n);i+=2){
	        if(p[i]){
	            for(int j=i*i;j<=n;j+=2*i){
	                p[j] = 0;
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    return p;
	}
	
	ll power(ll x, ll y, ll m){
		if(y==0)
			return 1;
		ll smallpower = power(x,y/2,m);
		smallpower = smallpower%m;
		smallpower = (smallpower*smallpower)%m;
		if(y&1)
	         return (x*smallpower)%m;
		else
			return (smallpower%m);
	}

11/05/2020, 00:10 - Kunal Farmah: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

class Hero{
public:

    int p,q,v;
    Hero(int a, int b, int c){
      p=a;q=b;v=c;
    }
    bool operator<(Hero a){
      return a.v>this->v && a.p>this->p && a.q>this->q;
    }
};

bool compare(Hero a, Hero b){
  if(a.v==b.v){
    if(a.q==b.q){
      return a.p<b.p;
    }
    return a.q<b.q;
  }
  return a.v<b.v;
}

class compareV{
public:bool operator()(int x,Hero b ) {
      return x < b.v;
    }
};
class compareQ{
public:bool operator()(int x,Hero b ) {
      return x < b.q;
    }
};
class compareP{
public:bool operator()(int x,Hero b ) {
      return x < b.p;
    }
};

int main()
{
  int t;
  cin>>t;

  while(t--){
    int n;
    cin>>n;

    int P[n],Q[n],V[n];
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
      cin>>P[i];
    }
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
      cin>>Q[i];
    }
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
      cin>>V[i];
    }

    vector<Hero> heros;
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
      Hero h = Hero(P[i],Q[i],V[i]);
      heros.push_back(h);
    }

    sort(heros.begin(),heros.end(),compare);
    int c=0;
    for(int i=0; i<heros.size(); i++){
      auto it1 = upper_bound(heros.begin(),heros.end(),heros[i].v,compareV());
      auto it2 = upper_bound(heros.begin(),heros.end(),heros[i].q,compareQ());
      auto it3 = upper_bound(heros.begin(),heros.end(),heros[i].p,compareP());
      // take the first hero u find and remove him
      auto it = max(it1,min(it2,it3));
      // while(it<heros.end() && (it->p<=heros[i].p || it->v  <= heros[i].v || it->q<=heros[i].q) ){
      //   ++it;
      // }
      if(heros[i]<*it) {
        c++;
        heros.erase(heros.begin() + i);
        --i;
      }
    }

    cout<<c<<endl;
  }

  return 0;
}

Nick Fury provides you with the records and asks you to find the

11/05/2020, 00:10 - Kunal Farmah: /*Many Evil Souls on the Earth are waiting for salvation. Now God has incarnated on the Earth to liberate those souls.
There are N number of souls on the Earth and also the value of bad deeds 
V[i] of all souls is given. Now to get salvation from god all the souls 
come one-by-one in a queue in front of God.

God selects the soul one-by-one from the start and compares its 
V[i] value with the minimum value of bad deed of all the souls. 
If both are the same, then God gives salvation to that soul. 
Otherwise, he sends that soul to the end of the queue to get another chance. 
This process continues until all souls get salvation.

You have to determine the total number of times God needs to 
perform the operation until all souls receive salvation.*/

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main()
{
  int n;
  cin>>n;
  queue<int>q;
  int minval = INT_MAX;
  unordered_map<int,int> m;
  
  // map<int,int> m;
  // for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
  //   int x;
  //   cin>>x;
  //   m[x]=i;
  // }
  // int ans=0;
  // auto i = m.begin();
  // int prev = i->second;
  // ++i;
  // for(;i!=m.end();i++){
  //   // for(int ind : i){
  //   ans+=(abs(i->second-prev)+1);
    
  //   // }
  //   prev= i->second;
  // }
  // cout<<ans<<endl;

  set<int> s;
  for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
    int x;
    cin>>x;
    minval = min(minval,x);
    q.push(x);
    s.insert(x);
    m[x]++;
  }

  minval = *s.begin();
  int c=0;
  while(!q.empty()){
    int x = q.front();
    q.pop();
    ++c;
    if(x!=minval){
      q.push(x);
    }
    else{
      --m[minval];
      if(m[minval]==0){
        s.erase(s.begin());
        minval = *s.begin();
      }
    }
  }

  cout<<c<<endl;
  return 0;
}

class hero{
public:
	long int power, villiansDefeated, intellect;
};

int main(){
   IOS;
 /*    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
         freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
         freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
     #endif */
   
   long int n;
   cin>>n;

   vector<hero> v(n);

   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
   		cin>>v[i].power;

   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
   		cin>>v[i].villiansDefeated;

   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
   		cin>>v[i].intellect;

   sort(v.begin(),v.end(),[](hero a, hero b){
   		if(a.power != b.power)
   			a.power < b.power;

   		if(a.intellect != b.intellect)
   			a.intellect > b.intellect;

   		return a.villiansDefeated < b.villiansDefeated;
   });


   map<long int,long int> m;

   m[1e9] = -1e9;
   m[-1e9] = 1e9;


   long int ans = 0;
   for(long int i = n - 1; i >= 0; i--){
   		auto it = m.upper_bound(v[i].intellect);

   		if(it->second > v[i].villiansDefeated)
   			ans++;

   		else if(m[v[i].intellect] < v[i].villiansDefeated){
   			m[v[i].intellect] = v[i].villiansDefeated;
   			for(auto itr = --m.lower_bound(v[i].intellect);itr->second < v[i].villiansDefeated;)
   				m.erase(itr--);
   		}
   }

   cout<<ans;

   return 0;
}

   	  cin>>v[i].first;
   	  v[i].second = i + 1;
   }

   sort(v.begin(),v.end());
   list<long int> l;

   for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
   		l.push_back(v[i].second);

   long int ans = 0;
   while(l.size()){
   		auto cur = l.front();
   		while(l.size() && cur <= l.front()){
   			cur = l.front();
   			l.pop_front();
   			ans++;
   		}
   		ans += l.size();
   }

   cout<<ans;


   return 0;
}

12/05/2020, 20:48 - Dhruv(DTU): #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
#define long long long 
vector<bool> isPrime; 

void sieve(long int n){
  isPrime.assign(n + 1,true);
  isPrime[0] = isPrime[1] = false;

  for(long int i = 2; i < isPrime.size(); i++){
    if(isPrime[i]){
      for(long int j = i*i; j < isPrime.size(); j += i)
        isPrime[j] = false;
    }
  }
}

long int dp[(long int)2e5+5];
long int n;
string s;

const long int MOD = 1e9 + 7;

long int solve(long int idx){
  if(idx >= n)
    return 1;
  
  if(dp[idx] != -1)
    return dp[idx];

    if(s[idx] == '0')
      return 0;

  long int ans = 0, num = 0;

  for(long int i = idx; i < n; i++){
      num = num * 10 + (s[i] - '0');
      
      if(num > 1e6)
        break;
      if(isPrime[num])
          ans = (ans + solve(i + 1)) % MOD;
      
  }

  return dp[idx] = ans % MOD;
}

int main(){
   
    sieve(1e6 + 1);
    memset(dp,-1,sizeof(dp));

    cin>>s;
    n = s.size();

    cout<<solve(0);
   return 0;
}

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

// Complete the ContestWinner function below.
// For your reference:
typedef struct node
{
    int value;
    struct node* next;
}node;

struct node* ContestWinner(struct node *head, int M, int size)
{
    node* temp = head;
    //node* prev = temp;
    while(temp->next){
        int k=0;
        while(k<M-2){
            temp=temp->next;
            ++k;
        }
        if(temp->next->next==temp){
            head=temp;
            break;
        }
        temp->next=temp->next->next;
        temp=temp->next;
    }
    return head;
}




int main(){

    int n,k;
    cin>>n>>k;

    int a;
    cin>>a;
    node* list= new node();
    node* tail = new node();
    list->value=a;
    tail=list;
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
        int x;
        cin>>x;
        node* t = new node();
        t->value = x;
        t->next =NULL;
        tail->next= t;
        tail=tail->next;
    }
    tail->next=list;

    ContestWinner(list,k,n);

    return 0;
}

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

// Complete the ContestWinner function below.
// For your reference:
typedef struct node
{
    int value;
    struct node* next;
}node;

struct node* ContestWinner(struct node *head, int M, int size)
{
    node* temp = head;
    --size;
    //node* prev = temp;
    while(temp->next && size){
        int k=0;
        while(k<M-2){
            temp=temp->next;
            ++k;
        }
        // if we are removing head, increment it first
         if(temp->next==head){
             head=head->next;
         }
        temp->next=temp->next->next;
        --size;
        temp=temp->next;
    }
    return head;
}





int main(){

    int n,k;
    cin>>n>>k;

    int a;
    cin>>a;
    node* list= new node();
    node* tail = new node();
    list->value=a;
    tail=list;
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
        int x;
        cin>>x;
        node* t = new node();
        t->value = x;
        t->next =NULL;
        tail->next= t;
        tail=tail->next;
    }
    tail->next=list;

    ContestWinner(list,k,n);

    return 0;
}

17/05/2020, 23:26 - Kunal Farmah: // Kunal Farmah

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

// Complete the ContestWinner function below.
// For your reference:
typedef struct Node {
    int data;
    struct Node *next;
}Node;


Node* ArrangeSalary(Node* head, int X) {
    Node* tail = head;
    int n  = 0;
    while(tail->next){
        tail=tail->next;
        ++n;
    }
    ++n;
    // creating a circular linked list to maintain original order
    Node* circhead = tail;
    tail->next = head;


    Node* temp=head;
    Node* prev = head;
    while(--n){
        if(temp->data>=X){
            // greater element is placed at end
            // circular end is incremented after
            Node* t  =new Node();
            t->data=temp->data;
            t->next = circhead->next;
            circhead->next=t;
            circhead = circhead->next;
            // if head was greater, just increment it
            if(head==temp)
                head=head->next;
            // else remove the greater element
            else
                prev->next=prev->next->next;
        }
        prev=temp;
        temp=temp->next;
    }
    // breaking the chain
    circhead->next=NULL;
    return head;

}




int main(){

    int n,k;
    cin>>n>>k;

    int a;
    cin>>a;
    Node* list= new Node();
    Node* tail = new Node();
    list->data=a;
    tail=list;
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
        int x;
        cin>>x;
        Node* t = new Node();
        t->data = x;
        t->next =NULL;
        tail->next= t;
        tail=tail->next;
    }
    tail->next=NULL;

    ArrangeSalary(list,k);

    return 0;
}

17/05/2020, 23:36 - Dhruv(DTU): // Complete the ContestWinner function below.
// For your reference:
/*
typedef struct node
{
    int value;
    struct node* next;
}node;
 */

struct node* ContestWinner(struct node *head, int M, int size){
  set<pair<long int,long int>>s;

  long int idx = 0;
  // auto temp = head;
  while(size--){
    s.insert(make_pair(head->value,idx++));
    head = head->next;
    // if(temp == head)
    //   break;
  }
  
  auto begin = s.begin();
  while(s.size() > 1){
    long int cnt = 0;
    auto ele = s.begin();
    for(auto i = begin;true; ){
      cnt++;
      if(cnt == M){
        ele = i;
        i++;
        if(i == s.end())
          i  = s.begin();
        begin = i;
        break;
      }
        i++;
      if(i == s.end())
        i = s.begin();
    }
    s.erase(*ele);
  }
  
  node *ans = new node;
  ans->value = s.begin()->first;
  ans->next = NULL;
  return ans;
}

17/05/2020, 23:59 - Kunal Farmah: // Kunal Farmah

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

// Complete the ContestWinner function below.
// For your reference:
struct Node {
    char data;
    struct Node *next;
};


Node* ListDestruction(Node *head)
{
    while(head->next && head->next->data==head->data){
        head=head->next;
    }

    Node* prev=head->next;
    Node* temp=head->next->next;
    Node* preprev = head;

    while(temp && temp->next){
        while(temp->next && temp->data==temp->next->data){
            preprev=prev;
            prev=temp;
            temp=temp->next;
        }
        if(prev && temp && prev->data==temp->data){
            preprev->next=temp->next;
            prev = temp->next;
            if(temp->next)
            temp = temp->next->next;
        }

        if(prev && preprev && preprev->data==prev->data){
            head = temp;
            preprev=head;
            prev = temp->next;
            if(temp->next)
            temp=temp->next->next;
        }
        preprev=prev;
        prev=temp;
        temp=temp->next;
    }


    return head;

}




int main(){

    int n;
    cin>>n;

    char a;
    cin>>a;
    Node* list= new Node();
    Node* tail = new Node();
    list->data=a;
    tail=list;
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
        char x;
        cin>>x;
        Node* t = new Node();
        t->data = x;
        t->next =NULL;
        tail->next= t;
        tail=tail->next;
    }
    tail->next=NULL;

    ListDestruction(list);

    return 0;
}

21/05/2020, 19:36 - Dhruv(DTU): auto _ = [](){
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(0);
    cout.tie(0);
    return 0;
}();

class Solution {
public:
    int countSquares(vector<vector<int>>& matrix) {
        long int n = matrix.size();
        if(!n)
            return 0;
        long int m = matrix[0].size();
        if(!m)
            return 0;
        
        vector<vector<int>> dp(n,vector<int>(m));
        
        dp[0][0] = matrix[0][0];
        for(long int i = 1; i < n; i++)
            dp[i][0] = matrix[i][0] + dp[i - 1][0];
        
        for(long int i = 1; i < m; i++)
            dp[0][i] = matrix[0][i] + dp[0][i - 1];
        
        for(long int i = 1; i < n; i++){
            for(long int j = 1; j < m; j++){
                dp[i][j] = dp[i][j - 1] + dp[i - 1][j] - dp[i- 1][j- 1] + matrix[i][j]; 
            }
        }
        
        long int ans = 0;
        
        for(long int size = 1; size <= n; size++){
            long int expected = size * size;
            for(long int i = size - 1; i < n; i++){
                for(long int j = size - 1; j < m; j++){
                    long int num = dp[i][j] ;
                    if(i >= size)
                        num -=  dp[i - size][j];
                    if(j >= size)
                        num -=  dp[i][j - size];
                    if(i >= size && j >= size)
                        num += dp[i - size][j - size];
                    if(num == expected)
                        ans++;
                }
            }
        }
        return ans;
    }
};

#include <ext/pb_ds/assoc_container.hpp> 
#include <ext/pb_ds/detail/standard_policies.hpp>
#include <ext/rope>

using namespace std;
using namespace __gnu_pbds;
using namespace __gnu_cxx;

#define IOS ios::sync_with_stdio(0); cin.tie(0); cout.tie(0);
#define endl "\n"
#define long long long 
#define PI 3.141592653589793238

#pragma GCC target ("avx2")
#pragma GCC optimization ("O3")
#pragma GCC optimization ("unroll-loops")

#define TRACE
#ifdef TRACE
#define trace(...) __f(#__VA_ARGS__, __VA_ARGS__)
    template <typename Arg1>
    void __f(const char* name, Arg1&& arg1){
        cout << name << " : " << arg1 << endl;
        //use cerr if u want to display at the bottom
    }
    template <typename Arg1, typename... Args>
    void __f(const char* names, Arg1&& arg1, Args&&... args){
        const char* comma = strchr(names + 1, ','); cout.write(names, comma - names) << " : " << arg1<<" | ";__f(comma+1, args...);
    }
#else
#define trace(...)
#endif

typedef trie<string,null_type,trie_string_access_traits<>,pat_trie_tag,trie_prefix_search_node_update> pref_trie;
typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;
typedef cc_hash_table<long int,long int, hash<long int>, equal_to<long int>, direct_mask_range_hashing<long int>, 
hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;
typedef gp_hash_table<long int,long int> HashTable;

long int n,k;
string s;

long int solve(){
  vector<long int> nextOccupied(n);
  nextOccupied[n - 1] = 1e10;
  long int ans = 0;

  for(long int i = n - 2; i >= 0; i--){
    nextOccupied[i] = nextOccupied[i + 1];
    if(s[i + 1] == '1')
      nextOccupied[i] = i + 1;
  }

  long int lastOccupied = -1e10;
  for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
    if(s[i] == '1')
      lastOccupied = i;
    else{
      long int before = i - lastOccupied;
      long int after = nextOccupied[i] - i;

      if(before > k && after > k){
        ans++;
        lastOccupied = i;
      }
    }
  }

  return ans;


}

int main(){
   IOS;
 /*    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
         freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
         freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
     #endif */
   
  long int t;
  cin>>t;

  while(t--){
    cin>>n>>k;
    cin>>s;

    long int ans = solve();
    reverse(s.begin(),s.end());
    ans = max(ans,solve());

    cout<<ans<<endl;
  }  
   return 0;
}

typedef trie<string,null_type,trie_string_access_traits<>,pat_trie_tag,trie_prefix_search_node_update> pref_trie;
typedef tree<long int,null_type,less<long int>,rb_tree_tag,tree_order_statistics_node_update>ordered_set;

hash_standard_resize_policy<hash_exponential_size_policy<>, hash_load_check_resize_trigger<true>, true>> ht;
typedef gp_hash_table<long int,long int> HashTable;

const long int OFFSET = 10;

class BIT{
    unordered_map<long int,long int> vec;
    public:

        void update(long int idx, long int val){
            idx += OFFSET;
            for(; idx < 100; idx += idx & (-idx))
                vec[idx] += val;
        }

        long int query(long int b){
            b += OFFSET;
            long int result = 0;
            while(b){
                result += vec[b];
                b -= b & (-b);
            }
            return result;
        }
};

int main(){
   IOS;
 /*    #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
         freopen("in.txt",  "r",  stdin);
         freopen("out.txt", "w", stdout);
     #endif */
   
   long int t;
   cin>>t;

   while(t--){
    string s;
    cin>>s;

    vector<long int> freq(26);
    for(auto ele : s)
      freq[ele - 'a']++;

    priority_queue<pair<long int,long int>> pq;

    for(long int i = 0; i < 26; i++)
      pq.push(make_pair(i,freq[i]));

    long int n;
    cin>>n;

    vector<long int> v(n);
    for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++)
        cin>>v[i];

    string ans(n,'$');
    BIT tree,tree2;


    while(pq.size()){
      vector<long int> nice;
      for(long int i = 0; i < n; i++){
          if(ans[i] !=  '$')
            continue;
         
         char c = s[i];
         long int bigSum = tree.query(50) - tree.query(i);
         long int bigCnt = tree2.query(50) - tree2.query(i);
         long int effectiveSum = bigSum - bigCnt * i;
         long int smallSum = tree.query(i - 1);
         long int smallCnt = tree2.query(i - 1);
         effectiveSum += (smallCnt * i - smallSum);

         if(effectiveSum == v[i])
          nice.push_back(i);
      }

      while(pq.size()){
        auto ele = pq.top();
        pq.pop();
        if(ele.second >= nice.size()){
          for(auto e : nice){
             tree.update(e,e);
             tree2.update(e,1);
            ans[e] = ele.first + 'a';
          }
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    cout<<ans<<endl;


   }
   return 0;
 }

03/08/2020, 12:38 - Dhruv(DTU): An array is given to you which contains only integer elements.  Moreover its guaranteed that sum of all elements in array is zero. In one move you can move some value from one index to any of its neighboring index. In case you're at index i then index i-1 and i+1 are your neighboring index.  You can consider array to be circular so last and first index are also neighbouring.   


Say take example of these test cases 


1 1 -2 

Now ans here is 2 I moved value from 2nd to 3rd index and  value from 1st to 3rd index cost is 2 


Similarly 1 2 3 -6
 Here answer is 3 I moved 
2nd value to 3rd index 
3rd index value to 4th index 
1st index value to 4th index 



Tell the minimum steps required to make whole array basically all emblems of arrays to 0

16/09/2020, 10:10 - Dhruv(DTU): #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

#define long long long 

int main(){
  
   
   string s;
   cin>>s;

   char last = '$';
   long int cnt = 0;
   string ans;

   for(long int i = 0; i < s.size(); i++){
      if(s[i] == last){
        cnt++;
      }
      else{
        if(cnt > 1){
          ans.push_back(last);
          ans.append(to_string(cnt));
          last = s[i];
          cnt = 1;
        }
        else if(cnt == 1){
          ans.push_back(last);
          last = s[i];
          cnt = 1;
        }
      }
   }

   if(cnt  > 1){
      ans.push_back(last);
      ans.append(to_string(cnt));
   }

   else if(cnt == 1){
      ans.push_back(last);
   }

   cout<<ans;


   return 0;
}
16/09/2020, 10:10 - Dhruv(DTU): #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;


#define long long long 

long int dp[201][201][201];
long int n,k;
   
long int solve(long int idx,long int groups, long int last){
	
	if(groups > k)
		return 0;

	if(idx == n){
		if(groups != k)
			return 0;
		return 1;
	}

	if(dp[idx][groups][last] != -1)
		return dp[idx][groups][last];

	long int ans = 0;

	for(long int i = idx; i < n; i++){
		long int included =  i - idx + 1;
		if(included >= last)
			ans += solve(i + 1, groups + 1, included);
	}	

	return dp[idx][groups][last] = ans;

}


int main(){
  
   cin>>n>>k;

   for(long int i = 0; i <= n; i++){
   		for(long int j = 0; j <= k; j++){
   			for(long int m = 0; m <= 200; m++){
   				dp[i][j][m] = -1;
   			}
   		}
   }

   cout<<solve(0,0,0);
   return 0;
}
